          <script class="use-script-element" type="text/javascript">
           (function(self) {
    if (self != window) {
      var wrapper = $(self)
        .closest('.section')
        .addClass('home-page-covid-banner');
      var clone = wrapper.find('> .row > .span24 >div:not(.molecule-999)').clone();
      var newRow = $('<div />', {
        class:
          'home-page-covid-banner section full layout-1280 preserve-row-content stickable-row visible-when-sticky',
      });
      newRow
        .append($('<div />', { class: 'row' }))
        .find('.row')
        .append(clone);
      wrapper.after(newRow);
      if (isIE()) {
        newRow.addClass('ie');
        wrapper.addClass('ie');
      }
      var mols501 = wrapper.find('.molecule-lb-501').add(newRow.find('.molecule-lb-501'));
      mols501.each(function() {
        var img = $(this).find('.clf img');
        var clf = img.parent();
        var src = img.attr('src');
        var cta = $(this).find('.button');
        clf.css({
          'background-image': 'url(' + src + ')',
        });
        cta
          .on('mouseenter', function() {
            clf.addClass('active');
          })
          .on('mouseleave', function() {
            clf.removeClass('active');
          });
      });
      function isIE() {
        var ua = window.navigator.userAgent;
        var msie = ua.indexOf('MSIE ');
        if (msie > 0) {
          // IE 10 or older => return version number
          return parseInt(ua.substring(msie + 5, ua.indexOf('.', msie)), 10);
        }
        var trident = ua.indexOf('Trident/');
        if (trident > 0) {
          // IE 11 => return version number
          var rv = ua.indexOf('rv:');
          return parseInt(ua.substring(rv + 3, ua.indexOf('.', rv)), 10);
        }
        var edge = ua.indexOf('Edge/');
        if (edge > 0) {
          // Edge (IE 12+) => return version number
          return parseInt(ua.substring(edge + 5, ua.indexOf('.', edge)), 10);
        }
        // other browser
        return false;
      }
      $(self).remove();
    } else {
      var script = document.querySelector(' script.use-script-element');
      script.className = '';
      Function(script.innerHTML).call(script);
    }
  })(this);
          </script>
         </div>

          <script class="use-script-element" type="text/javascript">
           ;(function(self) {
    if (self != window) {
      var m705 = $(self).closest('.span24').find('.molecule-lb-705').removeClass('molecule-lb-705');
      
      function BGVideo(el) {
        var self = this;
        var customBGColor = el.closest('.section').find('.molecule-lb-501').attr('data-custom-value-1');
        var bgImgHelper = el.closest('.section').find('.bg-img-helper').addClass('bg-video-helper');
        var mediaTablet = window.matchMedia('screen and (max-width: 1279px)');
        var mediaMobile = window.matchMedia('screen and (max-width: 719px)');

        if (customBGColor) {
          bgImgHelper.addClass('custom-bg').css('background-color', customBGColor);
        }

        /*el.closest('.section').find('.molecule-lb-501').addClass('clickable-link-desktop');*/
        bgImgHelper.html('<div class="ratio-helper"></div>');

        this.init = function() {
          var tabletVideo = el.find('.mobile[data-type="video"]').attr('data-src').split('||');
          this.videoWrapper = el.find('.ambient-video-wrapper');
          this.config = {};
          this.config.desktop = el.find('.desktop[data-type="video"]').attr('data-src');
          this.config.tablet = tabletVideo[0];
          this.config.mobile = tabletVideo.length > 1 ? tabletVideo[1] : tabletVideo[0];

          this.update();
          this.initListeners();
        }

        this.initVideo = function(size) {
          var currentVideo = bgImgHelper.find('video');
          if (currentVideo.length) {
            currentVideo.remove();
          }
          bgImgHelper.prepend(this.getVideoTpl(this.config[size]));
          this.video = bgImgHelper.find('video')[0];
          this.video.addEventListener('loadedmetadata', function() {
            self._initAspectRatio(self.video.videoWidth, self.video.videoHeight);
          });
        }

        this._initAspectRatio = function(width, height) {
          this.ratio = width / height;
          $(window).on('resize', _.debounce(function() {
            self._calcVideoWidth();
          }, 100));
          this._calcVideoWidth();
        }

        this._calcVideoWidth = function() {
          let minWidth = this.ratio * bgImgHelper.height();
          $(this.video).css('min-width', minWidth);
        }

        this.getVideoTpl = function(src) {
          if (src) {
            return '<video muted autoplay playsinline loop>' +
                     '<source src="' + src + '" type="video/mp4">'+
                   '</video>'
          } else {
            console.warn('check 705 setup')
          }
        }

        this._getCurrentMedia = function() {
          var platform = 'desktop';
          if (mediaTablet.matches) {
            platform = mediaMobile.matches ? 'mobile' : 'tablet';
          }
          return platform;
        }

        this.initListeners = function() {
          $(window).on('resize', _.debounce(function() {
            var video = bgImgHelper.find('video');
          }, 100));

          mediaTablet.addListener(self.update);
          mediaMobile.addListener(self.update);
        }

        this.update = function() {
          var current = self._getCurrentMedia();
          self.initVideo(current);
        }

        if (!el.find('.desktop[data-src="#"]').length) {
          this.init()
        } else {
          el.closest('.section').addClass('use-video-layout');
        }
      }

      new BGVideo(m705);
      $(self).remove();
      m705.remove();
    } else {
      var script = document.querySelector('script.use-script-element');
      script.className = '';
      Function(script.innerHTML).call(script);
    }
  })(this);
          </script>
         </div>

          <script class="use-script-element" type="text/javascript">
           ;(function(scriptEl) {
                          if (scriptEl != window) {

                            var AutoSlider = function() {
                              var self = this;
                              var customDuration = 'duration-10000';
                              var timerTimeout;
                              var tabletMedia = window.matchMedia('screen and (max-width: 1279px)');
                              var mobileMedia = window.matchMedia('screen and (max-width: 719px)');
                              var mobileMediaS = window.matchMedia('screen and (max-width: 330px)');

                              this.init = function() {
                                this.initSlider();
                              }
                              this.initSlider = function() {
                                this.slider = $(scriptEl).closest('.flex-content');
                                $(scriptEl).remove();
                                this.slider.addClass('bulleted-dots auto-slider').on('beforeChange', function(event, slick, from, to) {
                                  setTimeout(function() {
                                    self.pauseTimer(true);
                                    self.syncDots();
                                  });
                                }).on('afterChange', function(event, slick, to) {
                                  var slideHasVideo = slick.$slides.eq(to).find('video').length;
                                  self.dots.find('.play-btn').removeClass('paused');
                                  self.startTimer(slideHasVideo ? customDuration : '');
                                  self.restartBGVideo(slick.$slides, to);
                                }).on('init', function(e, slick) {
                                  var currentSlideEl = slick.$slides.eq(0);
                                  setTimeout(function() {
                                    var video = currentSlideEl.find('video').first();
                                    self.initTimer();
                                    self.updateDots();
                                    if (video.length) {
                                      if (video[0].readyState !== 4) {
                                        video[0].addEventListener('loadedmetadata', function() {
                                          self.startTimer(customDuration);
                                        });
                                      } else {
                                        self.startTimer(customDuration);
                                      }
                                    } else {
                                      self.startTimer();
                                    }
                                    self.initListeners();
                                  });
                                }).slick({
                                  dots: true,
                                  touchMove: false,
                                  touchThreshold: 30,
                                  infinite: true,
                                  pauseOnFocus: false,
                                  pauseOnHover: false,
                                  fade: true,
                                  slide: '.section',
                                  arrows: false
                                });
                              }
                              this.initTimer = function() {
                                this.timerElParent = $('<div />', {
                                  class: 'slick-timer'
                                });
                                this.timerEl = $('<div />', {
                                  class: 'inner'
                                });
                                this.timerElParent.append(this.timerEl);
                                this.slider.append(this.timerElParent);
                                this.updateTimerYPos();
                              }
                              this.restartBGVideo = function(slides, current) {
                                var hiddenVideos = slides.filter(function(i) {
                                  return i !== current;
                                }).find('video').each(function() {
                                  this.pause();
                                  this.currentTime = 0.01;
                                });

                                var video = slides.eq(current).find('video').first();
                                if (video.length) {
                                  video[0].currentTime = 0.01;
                                  video[0].play();
                                }
                              }
                              this.updateDots = function() {
                                this.dots = $('<div />', {
                                  class: 'controls'
                                });
                                this.pauseBtn = $('<a href="#" class="play-btn"><div class="left"></div><div class="right"></div><div class="t-1"></div><div class="t-2"></div></a>');
                                this.dots.append(this.pauseBtn);
                                this.slider.append(this.dots);
                                this.syncDots();
                              }
                              this.syncDots = function() {
                                var dots = this.slider.find('> .slick-dots').clone();
                                dots.find('button').each(function() {
                                  $(this).attr('data-id', $(this).attr('id')).removeAttr('id');
                                })
                                this.dots.find('>.slick-dots').remove();
                                this.dots.append(dots);
                              }
                              this.initListeners = function() {
                                $(window).on('resize', _.debounce(function() {
                                    self.updateTimerYPos();
                                }, 100));
                                /*this.timerElParent.on('mouseenter', function() {
                                  self.pauseTimer();
                                });
                                this.timerElParent.on('mouseleave', function() {
                                  self.resumeTimer();
                                });*/
                                this.timerElParent.on('animationend', function() {
                                  self.slideNext();
                                });
                                this.dots.on('click', 'button', function() {
                                  $('#' + $(this).attr('data-id')).click();
                                });
                                this.slider.on('mouseenter', 'a.button', function() {
                                  self.pauseTimer();
                                }).on('mouseleave', 'a.button', function() {
                                  if (!self.dots.find('.play-btn').hasClass('paused')) {
                                    self.resumeTimer();
                                  }
                                });
                                this.dots.find('.play-btn').on('click', function(e) {
                                  e.preventDefault();
                                  if ($(this).hasClass('paused')) {
                                    self.resumeTimer();
                                    $(this).removeClass('paused');
                                  } else {
                                    self.pauseTimer();
                                    $(this).addClass('paused');
                                  }
                                });
                              }
                              this.updateTimerYPos = function() {
                                this.timerElParent.css('top', this.slider.find('.bg-img-helper:first').outerHeight() - 4);
                              }
                              this.startTimer = function(customDurationClass) {
                                customDurationClass = customDurationClass || '';
                                self.timerElParent.removeClass('playing paused ' + customDuration);
                                setTimeout(function() {
                                  self.timerElParent.addClass('playing ' + customDurationClass);
                                });
                              }
                              this.pauseTimer = function(restart) {
                                this.timerElParent.addClass('paused');
                                restart && this.timerElParent.removeClass('playing');
                              }
                              this.resumeTimer = function() {
                                this.timerElParent.removeClass('paused');
                              }
                              this.slideNext = function() {
                                this.slider.slick('slickNext');
                              }

                              this.init();
                            }

                            var PrefixMainBannerMetrics = function() {
                              var ROWs = $(scriptEl).closest('.flex-content').find('.section');
                              ROWs.each(function(i, row) {
                                $(this).find('.flex2-molecule').filter(function() {
                                  return $(this).attr('data-metrics-title');
                                }).each(function() {
                                  var defaulTitle = $(this).attr('data-metrics-title');
                                  var regexp = new RegExp(/^s\d/);
                                  if (defaulTitle && !regexp.test(defaulTitle)) {
                                    var prefix = 's1.' + (i + 1) + '_';
                                    $(this).attr('data-metrics-title', prefix + defaulTitle);
                                  }
                                });
                              });
                            }

                            new PrefixMainBannerMetrics();

                            new AutoSlider();
                          } else {
                            var script = document.querySelector('script.use-script-element');
                            script.className = '';
                            Function(script.innerHTML).call(script);
                          }
                        }
                        )(this);
          </script>
         </div>
         <!--FLEX2: End flex-mol-999-tcm245-2899421 molecule-999 flex2-molecule-->
        </div>

          <script class="use-script-element" type="text/javascript">
           ;(function(scriptEl) {
    if (scriptEl != window) {
      var mainPart = $('#home-content').addClass('category-drawer');
      lastCont = $(scriptEl).parents('.flex-content').addClass('hide-content category-drawer-content last-product-var category-drawer');
      mainPart.nextUntil('.flex-content.last-product-var').addClass('hide-content category-drawer-content category-drawer');
      var content = $('.category-drawer-content')
        , moduleParts = $('.category-drawer')
        , stickyRow = content.find('.stickable-row').removeClass('stickable-row').addClass('stick-row')
        , stickyChilds = stickyRow.find('> .row:first-child');

      var enableHash = true;
      var stickyElsAbove = $();

      function init() {
        setIDs();
        appendIcons();
        initListeners();

        $(function() {
          setTimeout(function() {
            initStickable();
            (enableHash) && checkURLParams();
          });
        });
      }

      function initStickable() {
        var stickyElsSelector = '.home-page-stickable-banner, .stickable-row';

        stickyRow.first().closest('.section')
           .prevAll('.section')
           .find(stickyElsSelector).first().each(function() {
             stickyElsAbove = $(this);
           });

        if (!stickyElsAbove.length) {
          stickyRow.first().closest('.flex-content')
             .prevAll('.flex-content')
             .find(stickyElsSelector).first().each(function() {
               stickyElsAbove = $(this);
             });
        }
        stickyRow.each(function() {
          new GLOBALS.Stickable($(this).find('>.row:first-child'), $(this), {fixedElAbove: stickyElsAbove});
          alignHeights($(this).find('>.row:first-child'), $(this));
        });
      }

      function alignHeights(el, parent) {
        updateHeight(el, parent);
        function updateHeight(el, parent) {
          parent.height(el.outerHeight());
        }
        $(window).on('resize load', _.throttle(function() {
          updateHeight(el, parent);
        }, 100));
      }

      function setIDs() {
        var triggers = mainPart.find(".molecule-lb-502 .link-lists a");
        triggers.each(function(index, el) {
          var id = $(el).attr('href').replace('#', '');
          $(content.eq(index)).attr('id', id);
        });
      }

      function appendIcons() {
        mainPart.find('.molecule-lb-502').each(function() {
          var link = $(this).find('.link-lists a');
          link.after('<div class="icon-plus"></div>');
        });
      }

      function isActive(el) {
        var parent = el.parents('.category-drawer-content');
        return parent.hasClass('hide-content') ? false : true;
      }

      function getScrollTo(contentEl) {
        var stickRow = contentEl.find('.stick-row');
        if (stickRow.length) {
          var scrollTo = stickRow.offset().top;
        } else {
          var scrollTo = contentEl.offset().top;
        }
        if (stickyElsAbove.length) {
          scrollTo -= stickyElsAbove.outerHeight();
        }
        return scrollTo;
      }

      function initListeners() {
        mainPart.find('.molecule-lb-502').on('click', function() {
          console.log('CLICK 1');
          $(this).find('.link-lists a').trigger('click');
        });

        mainPart.find('.molecule-lb-502 .link-lists a').on('click', function(event, data) {
          console.log('CLICK 2');
          event.preventDefault();
          event.stopPropagation();
          var id = $(event.currentTarget).attr('href').replace('#', '');
          var contentEl = $('#' + id);
          moduleParts.addClass('hide-content');
          contentEl.removeClass('hide-content');

          if (contentEl.length) {
            var scrollTo = getScrollTo(contentEl);
            
            if (enableHash && !data) {
              GLOBALS.Hash.set({
                'catdrawer': id
              }, true);
            }
            var duration = (enableHash && data && data.noanimation) ? 0 : 300;
            GLOBALS.ScrollTo._scrollToMobile(scrollTo, duration);
          } else {
            console.log('Error! Wrong content id.');
          }
          $(event.currentTarget).trigger('sendmetrics');

          return false;
        });

        stickyRow.find('a').on('click', function(event) {
          console.log('CLICK 3');
          event.preventDefault();
          var id = $(event.currentTarget).attr('href').replace('#', '');
          var contentEl = $('#' + id);

          moduleParts.addClass('hide-content');
          contentEl.removeClass('hide-content');

          if (contentEl.length) {
            if (enableHash) {
              GLOBALS.Hash.set({
                'catdrawer': (id == 'home-content') ? '' : id
              }, true);
            }

            var scrollTo = getScrollTo(contentEl);
            if (scrollTo < $(window).scrollTop()) {
              window.scrollTo(0, scrollTo);
            }
          }
        });

        $(window).on('scroll', _.throttle(checkOnScrol, 150));

        function checkOnScrol() {
          var visibleContent = content.filter(':not(.hide-content)');
          if (visibleContent.length) {
            var additionalHeight = stickyElsAbove.length ? stickyElsAbove.outerHeight() : 0;
            if (visibleContent[0].getBoundingClientRect().bottom < 40 + additionalHeight) {
              stickyChilds.addClass('hidden');
            } else {
              stickyChilds.removeClass('hidden')
            }
          }
        }
      }

      function checkURLParams() {
        var openedDrawer = GLOBALS.Hash.get('catdrawer');

        if (openedDrawer) {
          $('[href="#' + openedDrawer + '"]:not(.clickable-overlay)', mainPart).trigger('click', {
            noanimation: true
          });
        }
      }

      init();

      function PrefixSecondaryBannerMetrics() {
        var ROWs = content;
        ROWs.each(function() {
          $(this).find('.section.custom-mobile-width .flex2-molecule.molecule-lb-502').each(function(i) {
            var defaulTitle = $(this).attr('data-metrics-title');
            var regexp = new RegExp(/^t\d/);
            if (defaulTitle && !regexp.test(defaulTitle)) {
              var prefix = 't' + (i + 1) + '_';
              $(this).attr('data-metrics-title', prefix + defaulTitle);
            }
          });
        });
      }

      PrefixSecondaryBannerMetrics();

    } else {
      var script = document.querySelector('script.use-script-element');
      script.className = '';
      Function(script.innerHTML).call(script);
    }
  }
  )(this);
          </script>
         </div>
         <!--FLEX2: End flex-mol-999-tcm245-2900192 molecule-999 flex2-molecule-->
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>

          <script class="use-script-element" type="text/javascript">
           ;(function(scriptEl){
                    if (scriptEl != window) {
                      var variation = $(scriptEl).closest('.flex-content').addClass('variation-search');
                      var form = $(scriptEl).closest('.flex2-molecule').find('.variation-search-form');

                      form.find('.button').on('click', function(e, data) {
                        if (!data) {
                          form.trigger('submit', {custom: true});
                        }
                      });
                      form.on('submit', function(e, data) {
                        if (!data) {
                          //submit is triggered via clicking on a submit link
                          form.find('.button').trigger('click', {custom: true});
                        }

                        e.preventDefault();
                        var searchQuery = $.trim(form.find('input[type="text"]').val());

                        if (searchQuery) {
                          window.location.href = getSearchUrl(searchQuery);
                        }
                      });

                      function getSearchUrl(query) {
                        //en-us
                        //https://www8.hp.com/us/en/search/search-results.html?ajaxpage=1#/page=1&/qt=elite
                        var lang = $('html').attr('lang').split('-');
                        var cc = lang[1];
                        var lc = lang[0];
                        return 'https://www8.hp.com/' + cc + '/' + lc + '/search/search-results.html?ajaxpage=1#/page=1&/qt=' + query;
                      }
                    } else {
                      var script = document.querySelector('script.use-script-element');
                      script.className = '';
                      Function(script.innerHTML).call(script);
                    }
                  })(this);
          </script>
